Version = 0.1

SS-0 [Meta]
    Bash $$ - Most Likely Always Requires Administrator (CMD)
    Powershell $$ - Most Likely Always Requires Administrator (PS1)
    ** - Requires Restart
    ! - Delete Parent Folder As Well
    ~ - An Action / Child of Parent
    # - A Note/Comment
    + - A Parent / Text Entry Signal
    @Powershell $$
        + takeown /F "_FOLDERNAME_" /R /D Y
            ~ # Takes Ownership of Folder
        + icacls "_FOLDERNAME_" /grant _USERNAME_:F /T
            ~ # Grants Premissions Over Folder
        + rmdir /S /Q "_FILENAME_"
            ~ # Deletes Folder
        + Set-ExecutionPolicy RemoteSigned -Scope CurrentUser
            ~ # Sets PowerShell Execution Policy to Allow RemoteSign via CurrentUser
        + Get-AppxPackage *_APPNAME_* | Remove-AppxPackage
            ~ # Removes a Microsoft Package

    @Bash $$
        + dism /Online /Get-Features
            ~ # Displays Available Features

SS-1 [Environment]
    $$  [Unicode 65001 Set]**
        @BASH $$
            + chcp
               - # if not 65001
            + chcp 65001

        @Win+R > intl.cpl
            + Select >Administrator >Change System Locale
            + Check >> Beta: Use Unicode UTF-8
            * Reboot Required
